1 Apology epi dikasterion anabebeka ete gegonos ebdomekonta atekhnos oun xenos ekho tes enthade lexeos osper oun an ei to onti xenos etugkhanon on sunegignoskete depou an
1 Apology panton alogotaton oti oude ta onomata oion te auton eidenai kai eipein plen ei tis komodopoios tugkhanei on osoi de phthono kai diabole khromenoi umas
1 Apology peripheromenon phaskonta te aerobatein kai allen pollen phluarian phluarounta on ego ouden oute mega oute mikron peri epaio kai oukh os atimazon lego ten toiauten
1 Apology labein kai misthosasthai os emellen auto kalo te kagatho poiesein ten prosekousan areten en d an outos e ton ippikon tis e ton georgikon nun
1 Apology an ous arti elegon meizo tina e kat anthropon sophian sophoi eien e ouk ekho ti lego ou gar de egoge auten epistamai all ostis
1 Apology to manteion kai apophanon to khresmo oti outosi emou sophoteros esti su d eme ephestha diaskopon oun touton onomati gar ouden deomai legein en de
1 Apology ponous tinas ponountos ina moi kai anelegktos e manteia genoito meta gar tous politikous ea epi tous poietas tous te ton tragodion kai tous ton
1 Apology khresmou potera dexaimen an outos osper ekho ekhein mete ti sophos on ten ekeinon sophian mete amathes ten amathian e amphotera a ekeinoi ekhousin ekhein
1 Apology anthropon eidoton de oliga e ouden enteuthen oun oi up auton exetazomenoi emoi orgizontai oukh autois kai legousin os sokrates tis esti miarotatos kai diaphtheirei
1 Apology peirasomai apologesasthai authis gar de osper eteron touton onton kategoron labomen au ten touton antomosian ekhei de pos ode sokrate phesin adikein tous te neous
1 Apology de oi de akroatai beltious poiousin e ou kai outoi ti de oi bouleutai kai oi bouleutai all ara o melete me oi en te
1 Apology phere de poteron eme eisageis deuro os diaphtheironta tous neous kai poneroterous poiounta ekonta e akonta ekonta egoge ti deta o melete tosouton su emou
1 Apology kai tois andrasin toutoisi ego gar ou dunamai mathein poteron legeis didaskein me nomizein einai tinas theous kai autos ara nomizo einai theous kai ouk
1 Apology legein autos eauto en te graphe osper an ei eipoi adikei sokrates theous ou nomizon alla theous nomizon kaitoi touto esti paizontos sunepiskepsasthe de o
1 Apology au oi daimones theon paides eisin nothoi tines e ek numphon e ek tinon allon on de kai legontai tis an anthropon theon men paidas
1 Apology dikaia e adika prattei kai andros agathou erga e kakou phauloi gar an to ge so logo eien ton emitheon osoi en troia teteleutekasin oi
1 Apology eisagoi tis eis dikasterion oti ou nomizo theous einai apeithon te manteia kai dedios thanaton kai oiomenos sophos einai ouk on to gar toi thanaton
1 Apology an umin oti ego umas o andres athenaioi aspazomai men kai philo peisomai de mallon to theo e umin kai eosper an empneo kai oios
1 Apology tauta ouden legei pros tauta phaien an o andres athenaioi e peithesthe anuto e me kai e aphiete me e me os emou ouk an
1 Apology genesetai o andres all ean emoi peithesthe pheisesthe mou umeis d isos takh an akhthomenoi osper oi nustazontes egeiromenoi krousantes an me peithomenoi anuto radios
1 Apology eu gar iste o andres athenaioi ei ego palai epekheiresa prattein ta politika pragmata palai an apolole kai out an umas opheleke ouden out an
1 Apology apothanoi oia de kai allois ekeinoi pollois polla prosetatton boulomenoi os pleistous anaplesai aition tote mentoi ego ou logo all ergo au enedeixamen oti emoi
1 Apology popote mathema mete edidaxa ei de tis phesi par emou popote ti mathein e akousai idia oti me kai oi alloi pantes eu iste oti
1 Apology adelphos outosi platon kai aiantodoros ou apollodoros ode adelphos kai allous pollous ego ekho umin eipein on tina ekhren malista men en to eautou logo
1 Apology anthropon oste kai oikeioi moi eisi kai ueis ge o andres athenaioi treis eis men meirakion ede duo de paidia all omos oudena auton deuro
1 Apology gar epi touto kathetai o dikastes epi to katakharizesthai ta dikaia all epi to krinein tauta kai omomoken ou kharieisthai ois an doke auto alla
1 Apology o andres athenaioi e delon oti tes axias ti oun t ti axios eimi pathein e apoteisai oti mathon en to bio oukh esukhian egon
1 Apology kai tes antiboleseos apauthadizomenos to de ouk estin o andres athenaioi toiouton alla toionde mallon pepeismai ego ekon einai medena adikein anthropon alla umas touto
1 Apology legontos emou akroasontai oi neoi osper enthade kan men toutous apelauno outoi me autoi exelosi peithontes tous presbuterous ean de me apelauno oi touton pateres
1 Apology einai ei kai me eimi oi boulomenoi umin oneidizein ei goun periemeinate oligon khronon apo tou automatou an umin touto egeneto orate gar de ten
1 Apology kai presbutes upo tou braduterou ealon oi d emoi kategoroi ate deinoi kai oxeis ontes upo tou thattonos tes kakias kai nun ego men apeimi
1 Apology ethelo to nuni moi sumbebekos ti pote noei emoi gar o andres dikastai umas gar dikastas kalon orthos an kaloien thaumasion ti gegonen e gar
1 Apology ei tina eklexamenon deoi tauten ten nukta en e outo katedarthen oste mede onar idein kai tas allas nuktas te kai emeras tas tou biou
1 Apology osper tous entautha diagein tis auton sophos estin kai tis oietai men estin d ou epi poso d an tis o andres dikastai dexaito exetasai
1 Charmides eggegonotes eien kai o kritias apoblepsas pros ten thuran idon tinas neaniskous eisiontas kai loidoroumenous allelois kai allon okhlon opisthen epomenon peri men ton kalon
1 Charmides ouk euprosopos uperphuos en d ego outos mentoi ephe ei etheloi apodunai doxei soi aprosopos einai outos to eidos pagkalos estin sunephasan oun kai oi
1 Charmides polun ekastos gar emon ton kathemenon sugkhoron ton plesion eothei spoude ina par auto kathezoito eos ton ep eskhato kathemenon ton men anestesamen ton de
1 Charmides estin en tois emeterois elikiotais memnemai de egoge kai pais on kritia tode sunonta se kalos ge su en d ego poion mallon gar soi
1 Charmides outos oude soma aneu psukhes alla touto kai aition eie tou diapheugein tous para tois ellesin iatrous ta polla nosemata oti tou olou ameloien ou
1 Charmides poioimen soi o phile kharmide akousas oun mou o kritias taut eipontos ermaion ephe o sokrates gegonos an eie e tes kephales astheneia to neanisko
1 Charmides ei de de kai pros sophrosunen kai pros talla kata ton toude logon ikanos pephukas makarion se en d ego o phile kharmide e meter
1 Charmides ope autos oiei beltion skepsasthai taute skopei tede toinun ephen ego dokei moi beltiste einai e skepsis peri autou delon gar oti ei soi parestin
1 Charmides ta tou kalou estin ta de bradea mogis te kai esukhe ta tou aiskhrou phainetai phainetai ara emin ephen ego kata ge to soma ou
1 Charmides ge toutou tou logou epeide kalon auton dei einai sophrona onta duoin gar de ta etera e oudamou emin e panu pou oligakhou ai esukhioi
1 Charmides eom od egog ephe estin ara os eoiken aidos ouk agathon kai agathon phainetai sophrosune de ge agathon eiper agathous poiei ois an pare kakous
1 Charmides kai ta ton philon onomata ouden etton e oun epolupragmoneite kai ouk esophroneite touto drontes oudamos kai men ou ta umetera ge auton eprattete eiper
1 Charmides upegela te kai eis ton kritian apeblepen kai o kritias delos men en kai palai agonion kai philotimos pros te ton kharmiden kai pros tous
1 Charmides prattein epeita ouden phesi koluein kai tous ta ton allon prattontas sophronein ego gar pou e d os touth omologeka os oi ta ton allon
1 Charmides opos su boulei onomazein tauten legeis su sophrosunen einai egoge ephe ouk ara sophronei o ta kaka pratton all o tagatha soi de e d
1 Charmides ephe o sokrates ouk an pote genoito all ei ti su oiei ek ton emprosthen up emou omologemenon eis touto anagkaion einai sumbainein ekeinon an
1 Charmides d ego saphes d ouden panu en on elegomen nun d ethelo toutou soi didonai logon ei me omologeis sophrosunen einai to gignoskein auton eauton
1 Charmides logistikes tekhnes e tes geometrikes ti estin toiouton ergon oion oikia oikodomikes e imation uphantikes e alla toiaut erga a polla an tis ekhoi pollon
1 Charmides men ti eidenai eidos de me kai nun de oun egoge phemi touto poiein ton logon skopein malista men emautou eneka isos de de kai
1 Charmides oti ouk oiden epeita ei oti malista dunaton tis an eie emin ophelia eidosin auto alla khre ephe skopein ithi de ephen ego o kritia
1 Charmides tas allas bouleseis bouletai ou gar oun erota de phaies an tina einai toiouton os tugkhanei on eros kalou men oudenos autou de kai ton
1 Charmides dunamin pros eauto ekhe ou kai ekeinen exei ten ousian pros en e dunamis autou en lego de to toionde oion e akoe phamen ouk
1 Charmides sophrosunen ophelimon ti kai agathon manteuomai einai su oun o pai kallaiskhrou tithesai gar sophrosunen tout einai epistemen epistemes kai de kai anepistemosunes proton men
1 Charmides oiden kai a me oiden oti o sokrates tauton estin touto ekeino isos ephen all ego kinduneuo aei omoios einai ou gar au manthano os
1 Charmides epistatai o phesin epistasthai e ouk epistatai alla tosouton monon os eoiken gnosetai oti ekhei tina epistemen otou de ge e sophrosune ou poiesei auton
1 Charmides anagke e oun aneu iatrikes dunait an tis touton poterois epakolouthesai ou deta oude ge allos oudeis os eoiken plen iatros oute de o sophron
1 Charmides kritia elegomen peri sophrosunes legontes oson agathon eie to eidenai a te oiden tis kai a me oiden panu men oun ephe outos nun de
1 Charmides emon a men isasin prattoien tauta a de me epistainto allois paradidoien tois epistamenois ouk oun ephe kalos omologesamen ou moi dokoumen en d ego
1 Charmides apotrepein tous de os alethos manteis kathistanai emin prophetas ton mellonton kateskeuasmenon de outo to anthropinon genos oti men epistemonos an prattoi kai zoe epomai
1 Charmides poion e d os petteutikon all e to logistikon oudamos all e to ugieinon mallon ephe ekeine d en lego malista en d ego e
1 Charmides monon estin kai anepistemosunes episteme allou de oudenos oukh outo phainetai ge ouk ara ugieias estai demiourgos ou deta alles gar en tekhnes ugieia e

1 Lysis o ge poneros to ponero oso an eggutero prosie kai mallon omile tosouto ekhthion gignesthai adikei gar adikountas de kai adikoumenous adunaton pou philous einai
1 Lysis philon oudamos alla de o men omoios to omoio ou philos o de agathos to agatho kath oson agathos ou kath oson omoios philos an

1 Theaetetus kai tois allois edoxan amatheis einai on eis gegonen aristeides o lusimakhou kai alloi panu polloi ous otan palin elthosi deomenoi tes emes sunousias kai
1 Theaetetus theaitete oti pot estin episteme peiro legein os d oukh oios t ei medepot eipes ean gar theos ethele kai andrize oios t ese alla

1 Theaetetus kai tripseos touto de kineseis e oukh autai geneseis puros autai men oun kai men to ge ton zoon genos ek ton auton touton phuetai
1 Theaetetus auto kath auto en on tithentes kai emin outo melan te kai leukon kai otioun allo khroma ek tes prosboles ton ommaton pros ten prosekousan
1 Theaetetus to dokoun pros ten nun erotesin apokrinomai oti ouk estin ean de pros ten proteran phulatton me enantia eipo oti estin eu ge ne ten
1 Theaetetus eniauto sou tou neou nun men meizo einai usteron de elatto meden tou emou ogkou aphairethentos alla sou auxethentos eimi gar de usteron o proteron

1 Theaetetus oper oromen te kai akouomen epistasthai phesomen ton men gar to skhema kai to khroma oran te kai epistasthai ton de ten oxuteta kai baruteta

0 XenophonHellenica1-3 tina kai ouk aition onta apokteinaite metamelesei de usteron anamnesthete os algeinon kai anopheles ede esti pros d eti kai peri thanatou anthropou emartekotes deina
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 pros ten anairesin me poiesantas a oi strategoi ekeleusan dioti ouk aneilonto krinesthai tosouton d ekho eipein uper amphoteron oti o kheimon diekoluse meden praxai
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 eteonikou stratiotai ontes eos men theros en apo te tes oras etrephonto kai ergazomenoi misthou kata ten khoran epei de kheimon egeneto kai trophen ouk
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 enestekoton pragmaton pempein eis lakedaimona presbeis tauta te erountas kai lusandron aitesontas epi tas naus eu pheromenon para tois summakhois kata ten proteran nauarkhian ote
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 en te samo kuros d epi toutois metepempsato lusandron epei auto para tou patros eken aggelos legon oti arroston ekeinon kaloie on en thamneriois tes
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 dierpasan oi stratiotai ousan plousian kai oinou kai sitou kai ton allon epitedeion plere ta de eleuthera somata panta apheke lusandros oi d athenaioi kata
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 strategein ouk ekeinon kai o men okheto lusandros d epei en emera pempte epipleousi tois athenaiois eipe tois par autou epomenois epan katidosin autous ekbebekotas
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 entautha de kategoriai egignonto pollai ton athenaion a te ede parenenomekesan kai a epsephismenoi esan poiein ei krateseian te naumakhia ten dexian kheira apokoptein ton
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 peisesthai nomizontes oia epoiesan melious te lakedaimonion apoikous ontas kratesantes poliorkia kai istiaieas kai skionaious kai toronaious kai aiginetas kai allous pollous ton ellenon te
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 ubrin edikoun anthropous mikropolitas oud epi mia aitia etera e oti ekeinois sunemakhoun dia tauta tous atimous epitimous poiesantes ekarteroun kai apothneskonton en te polei
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 katekhoi eita keleuoi eis lakedaimona ienai ou gar einai kurios on erototo up autou alla tous ephorous meta tauta erethe presbeutes eis lakedaimona autokrator dekatos
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 ekeinen ten emeran te elladi arkhein tes eleutherias kai o eniautos elegen en o mesounti dionusios o ermokratous surakosios eturannese makhe men proteron ettethenton upo
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 paradounai kai outos exelthon lusandros de tois arkhaiois politais paradous ten polin kai ta enonta panta kai deka arkhontas katastesas phrourein apheke to ton summakhon
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 erxanto bouleuesthai opos an exeie autois te polei khresthai opos boulointo ek toutou proton men pempsantes eis lakedaimona aiskhinen te kai aristotelen epeisan lusandron phrourous
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 ek toutou mentoi kritias kai oi alloi triakonta ede phoboumenoi kai oukh ekista ton theramenen me surrueiesan pros auton oi politai katalegousi triskhilious tous methexontas
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 einai to poiein o ti boulointo epibouleuousin auto kai idia pros tous bouleutas allos pros allon dieballon os lumainomenon ten politeian kai paraggeilantes neaniskois oi
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 epitithenai nun epei kai umeis kai emeis phaneros ekhthroi to demo gegenemetha ouket auto ta gignomena areskei opos autos men au en to asphalei kataste
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 toi estin os kai takhtheis anelesthai upo ton strategon tous kataduntas athenaion en te peri lesbon naumakhia autos ouk anelomenos omos ton strategon kategoron apekteinen
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 eauton kategorein ephainonto phaskontes gar oion te einai sosai tous andras proemenoi apolesthai autous apopleontes okhonto ou mentoi thaumazo ge to kritian paranenomekenai ote gar
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 kai ote ta opla tou plethous parerounto ou nomizon khrenai asthene ten polin poiein oude gar tous lakedaimonious eoron toutou eneka boulomenous perisosai emas opos
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 ego eimi oios aei pote metaballesthai katanoesate kai tauta ten men gar epi ton tetrakosion politeian kai autos depou o demos epsephisato didaskomenos os oi
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 egeneto eumenos epithorubesasa gnous o kritias oti ei epitrepsoi te boule diapsephizesthai peri autou anapheuxoito kai touto ou bioton egesamenos proselthon kai dialekhtheis ti tois
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 ton theramenen ekeinoi de eiselthontes sun tois uperetais egoumenou auton saturou tou thrasutatou te kai anaidestatou eipe men o kritias paradidomen umin ephe theramenen toutoni
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 os sun ebdomekonta phulen khorion katalambanei iskhuron oi de triakonta eboethoun ek tou asteos sun te tois triskhiliois kai sun tois ippeusi kai mal euemerias

0 XenophonHellenica1-3 te d usteraia oi men triakonta panu de tapeinoi kai eremoi sunekathento en to sunedrio ton de triskhilion opou ekastoi tetagmenoi esan pantakhou diepheronto pros

0 XenophonHellenica1-3 ep ephesou dia ton ellenidon poleon edomenos oti emellon opsesthai tas poleis en eirene eudaimonikos diagousas oi men de eporeuonto o de derkulidas epeide egno
0 XenophonHellenica1-3 e apekhei apo sardeon trion emeron odon kai mekhri toutou tou khronou en eirene diegon tissaphernes te kai derkulidas kai oi taute ellenes kai oi

0 XenophonHellenica1-3 suneideien autoi mentoi pasin ephasan suneidenai kai eilosi kai neodamodesi kai tois upomeiosi kai tois perioikois opou gar en toutois tis logos genoito peri spartiaton

0 XenophonHellenica1-3 ellenon epaisan tinas pantes sunetripsan ta dorata oi de persai kraneina palta ekhontes takhu dodeka men ippeas duo d ippous apekteinan ek de toutou etrephthesan

0 XenophonHellenica1-3 eis to katantes kai polle prothumia enekeinto etrephthesan oi thebaioi apo tou katantous kai apothneskousin auton pleious e diakosioi taute men oun te emera oi
